##############
# GUI Events #
##############
add_namespace = ottgui

country_event = { #Delete Irregular Divisions
	id = ottgui.1

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottgui.1 option 1"
		clr_country_flag = created_irregular_template
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Ottoman Irregulars" }
		every_state = { clr_state_flag = recruited_irregulars }
	}
}

country_event = { #cheat event for the AI (democratic path)
	id = ottgui.3

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottgui.3 option 1"
		### Add Turkish Nationalist votes in favour
		add_to_variable = { nat_tur_sup_deputies = 30 tooltip = nat_tur_sup_tt }

		### Add Arab Nationalist votes in favour
		add_to_variable = { nat_ara_sup_deputies = 30 tooltip = nat_ara_sup_tt }

		### Add Conservative votes in favour
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCCON } }
			}
			add_to_variable = { con_sup_deputies = 30 tooltip = con_sup_tt }
		}

		### Calculate coalition strength
		OTT_calc_coalition_strength = yes

		### cheat for marlib path
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
				has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCLIB }
				NOT = { has_government = social_liberal }
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.15
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #firing revolts that already passed the threshold
	id = ottgui.4

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottgui.4 option 1"
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				resistance > 70
			}
			OTT_launch_revolts = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Ottomans Turn the Tide
	id = ottgui.5
	title = ottgui.5.t
	desc = ottgui.5.d

	picture = GFX_OTT_Ottoman_Revolution

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_ai = yes
		OR = {
			has_war_with = EGY
			has_war_with = PER
		}
		NOT = { any_enemy_country = { is_ai = no } }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottgui.5 option ottgui.5.a"
		name = ottgui.5.a
		add_ideas = OTT_Ottoman_Reinvigoration
		every_army_leader = {
			add_temporary_buff_to_units = {
				combat_breakthrough = 0.20
				org_damage_multiplier = -0.30
				str_damage_multiplier = -0.30
				days = 100
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Kazim Karabekir unit event trigger
	id = ottgui.6

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_government = market_liberal
		social_liberal_plurality = yes
		has_completed_focus = OTT_Grand_Vizier_Sabahaddin
		has_completed_focus = OTT_Multi_Level_Democracy
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottgui.6 option 1"
		TUR_musa_kazim_karabekir = {
			add_temp_unit_leader_role = yes
			unit_leader_event = { id = ottlib.20 }
		}
	}
}

# Education Reform
country_event = {	#Education debate in the Meclis-i Mebusân
	id = ottpol.1
	title = ottpol.1.t
	desc = ottpol.1.d
	picture = GFX_OTT_Speech_Kemal

	trigger = {
		OTT_ottomans_have_post_defeat_content = no
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottpol.1 option ottpol.1.a"
		name = ottpol.1.a
		add_political_power = 30
		country_event = { id = ottpol.2 days = 10 }
	}
}

country_event = {	#Vote on the Education Decree
	id = ottpol.3
	title = ottpol.3.t
	desc = ottpol.3.d
	picture = GFX_OTT_Parliament

	trigger = {
		OTT_ottomans_have_post_defeat_content = no
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottpol.3 option ottpol.3.a"
		name = ottpol.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ott_edu_passed.tt
		country_event = { id = ottpol.4 days = 1 }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottpol.3 option ottpol.3.b"
		name = ottpol.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_ENDEAVOUR_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_ENDEAVOUR_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_NATPOP }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_PATAUT }
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		custom_effect_tooltip = ott_edu_refused.tt
		country_event = { id = ottpol.5 days = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = {	#Basis of the reformed code
	id = ottpol.7
	title = ottpol.7.t
	desc = ottpol.7.d

	picture = GFX_OTT_Desk_Kemal

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottpol.7 option ottpol.7.a"
		name = ottpol.7.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottpol.8 days = 7 }
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SWI
			modifier = OTT_adopted_civil_code
		}
		add_political_power = 30
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = ott_institutionalised_islam }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = ott_institutionalised_islam
				add_idea = ott_institutionalised_islam_spd
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottpol.7 option ottpol.7.b"
		name = ottpol.7.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottpol.8 days = 7 }
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AUS
			modifier = OTT_adopted_civil_code
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 183 #Cyprus
					state = 339 #Smyrna
					state = 585 #Batumi
				}
			}
			ott_decrease_revolt_risk = yes
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 554 #Damascus
					state = 754 #Medina
					state = 995 #Homs
				}
			}
			ott_decrease_revolt_risk = yes
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 352 #Van
					state = 812 #Basra
					state = 819 #Sulaymaniyah
				}
			}
			ott_decrease_revolt_risk = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = ott_institutionalised_islam }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = ott_institutionalised_islam
				add_idea = ott_institutionalised_islam_spd
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottpol.7 option ottpol.7.c"
		name = ottpol.7.c
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = OHF_tension_1 }
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ottpol.14 days = 2 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = reforms_blocked
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ottpol.8 days = 7 }
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { OTT_is_conservative_state = yes }
			ott_decrease_revolt_risk = yes
		}
	}
}

	id = ottpol.9
	title = ottpol.9.t
	desc = ottpol.9.d

	picture = GFX_OTT_Baghdad

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #New Elections Called
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottpol.9 option ottpol.9.a"
		name = ottpol.9.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			country_event = { id = ottpol.18 days = 30 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ott_elections
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = OHF_tension_2 }
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ottpol.30 days = 10 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ottpol.18 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	#Elections of [GetYear]
	id = ottpol.18
	title = ottpol.18.t
	desc = ottpol.18.d

	picture = GFX_OTT_Sheikh_Islam

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #OHF hold firm and gain supermajority
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottpol.18 option ottpol.18.a"
		name = ottpol.18.a
		trigger = {
			#NOT = { has_country_flag = mil_elections }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = OHF_tension_2 }
		}
		#ai_chance = { base = 40 }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_portraits = {
				character = TUR_mustafa_kemal_ataturk
				army = { large = GFX_portrait_TUR_mustafa_kemal_ataturk_civilian_large }
			}
			TUR_mustafa_kemal_ataturk = {
				add_temp_unit_leader_role = yes
				unit_leader_event = ottpol.19
			}
		}
	}
	#option = { #Military Intervention in Elections
	#	log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottpol.18 option ottpol.18.b"
	#	name = ottpol.18.b
	#	ai_chance = { base = 100 }

	#	}

	#		ideology = authoritarian_democrat
	#		popularity = 0.15
	#	}
	#	set_politics = {
	#		ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
	#	}
	#	hidden_effect = {

# Penal Code
country_event = {	#Status of the Alīye-i Emniyet Hizmeti
	id = ottpol.21
	title = ottpol.21.t
	desc = ottpol.21.d

	picture = GFX_OTT_Sublime_Porte1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottpol.21 option ottpol.21.a"
		name = ottpol.21.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc_lar = yes
				has_intelligence_agency = yes
			}
			add_ideas = ott_reformed_secret_service_lar
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_anti_partisan } }
				upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_anti_partisan
				add_political_power = -100
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_psycho_warfare } }
				upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_psycho_warfare
				add_political_power = -100
			}
			else = {
				add_political_power = -75
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc_lar = yes
				has_intelligence_agency = no
			}
			add_political_power = -100
			add_ideas = ott_reformed_secret_service_lar
			create_intelligence_agency = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -75
			add_ideas = ott_reformed_secret_service
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottpol.22 days = 200 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottpol.21 option ottpol.21.b"
		name = ottpol.21.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.025
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = OHF_tension_1
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ottpol.14 days = 3 } }
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ottpol.10 days = 3 } }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottpol.32 days = 200 }
		}
	}
}

	desc = ottpol.41.d

	#picture = GFX_OTT_Military_Academy

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottpol.41 option ottpol.41.a"
		name = ottpol.41.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
			name = TUR_military_government
			long_name = TUR_military_government_long
		}
		end_coalition = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottfev.1 days = 3 }
			country_event = { id = ottfev.6 days = 14 }
			news_event = ottnews.3
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = EGY
						is_core_of = SUD
						is_core_of = ARM
						is_core_of = LBA
						is_core_of = TRP
						is_core_of = YEM
						is_core_of = HEJ
					}
				}
				clear_occupy_state = yes
			}
		}
		load_focus_tree = ottoman_fevzi_focus
		complete_national_focus = OTT_State_of_Emergency
	}
}

country_event = {	#Sheikh Seyid Riza declares Jihad
	id = ottkem.33
	title = ottkem.33.t
	desc = ottkem.33.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OTT_ottomans_have_post_defeat_content = no
		OR = {
			352 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT } #Van
			354 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT } #Erzurum
			1000 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT } #Kars
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = OTT_conservative_revolt
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 352 #Van
						state = 354 #Erzurum
						state = 1000 #Kars
					}
				}
				add_core_of = KDR
				transfer_state_to = KDR
				teleport_armies = { to_state = THIS.capital }
			}
			KDR = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = OTT
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { controls_state = 345 } #Sivas
				KDR = {
					set_province_controller = 3890
					set_province_controller = 7620
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { controls_state = 350 } #Diyarbakir
				KDR = {
					set_province_controller = 7530
					set_province_controller = 11739
					set_province_controller = 11759
					set_province_controller = 13745
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { KDR = { controls_state = 352 } } #Van
				set_province_controller = 4583
				set_province_controller = 12476
			}
			if = {
				limit = { KDR = { controls_state = 354 } } #Erzurum
				set_province_controller = 9858
				set_province_controller = 9868
				set_province_controller = 11853
			}
			if = {
				limit = { KDR = { controls_state = 1000 } } #Kars
				set_province_controller = 10472
				set_province_controller = 13672
			}
			KDR = {
				KDR_spawn_revolt_units = yes
				country_event = kur.1
			}
			PER = { country_event = { id = ottfor.44 days = 7 } }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottkem.33 option ottkem.33.a"
		name = ottkem.33.a
	}
}

		}
	}

	option = { #You have no power here
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottkem.56 option ottkem.56.a"
		name = ottkem.56.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = ott_separated_church_state }
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = OTT_Mothers_of_the_Nation }
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = { OTT_is_conservative_state = yes }
				ott_increase_revolt_risk = yes
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = { OTT_is_conservative_state = yes }
				ott_increase_revolt_risk = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { OTT_is_conservative_state = yes }
				ott_increase_revolt_risk = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Why do they still have power here?
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottkem.56 option ottkem.56.b"
		name = ottkem.56.b
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ott_separated_church_state } }

			popularity = 0.125
		}
	}

			}

			idea = ott_receding_tide

		}

		name = ottkem.58.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				social_conservative > 0.49
				has_idea = ott_pluralist_constitution
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TUR_halide_edip_adivar = { is_hired_as_advisor = yes } }
			deactivate_advisor = TUR_halide_edip_adivar_advisor
		}
		add_stability = 0.10
		country_event = { id = ottkem.59 hours = 6 }
	}
}

		name = ottkem.59.a

		custom_effect_tooltip = ott_the_women_question_answered
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 0.15 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = ott_receding_tide
			years = 2
		}
		add_stability = -0.10
	}

	option = { #Sultan Vetos
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottkem.59 option ottkem.59.b"
		name = ottkem.59.b
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ott_no_veto } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = ott_the_women_question_answered
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 0.1 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = ott_receding_tide
			years = 2
		}
		add_stability = -0.20
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = TUR_abdulmecid_osmanoglu }
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = OTT_abdulmecid_score value = 1 }
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ottkem.66 days = 50 random_days = 10 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Passes
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottkem.59 option ottkem.59.c"
		name = ottkem.59.c
		trigger = { has_country_flag = ott_no_veto }
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = ott_the_women_question_backlash
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = ott_receding_tide
			years = 2
		}
		remove_ideas = ott_universal_suffrage
		retire_character = TUR_halide_edip_adivar
		clr_country_flag = ott_women_suffrage
	}
}

		}

		}
		184 = {
			ott_increase_revolt_risk = yes
		}

			limit = {

			OR = {

				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
		291 = {
			ott_increase_revolt_risk = yes
		}
		812 = {
			ott_increase_revolt_risk = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottsep.8 option ottsep.8.b"
		name = ottsep.8.b
		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
		add_political_power = -10
		if = {
			limit = { OTT_has_centralist_government = no }
			### Return Arab Nationalist votes to opposition
			subtract_from_variable = { nat_ara_sup_deputies = 10 tooltip = nat_ara_opp_tt }

			### Calculate coalition strength
			OTT_calc_coalition_strength = yes
		}
	}
}

	option = {

		hidden_effect = { LBA = { clear_all_relations = yes } }
		if = {
			limit = { OTT_has_centralist_government = no }
			### Return Arab Nationalist votes to opposition
			subtract_from_variable = { nat_ara_sup_deputies = 10 tooltip = nat_ara_opp_tt }

			### Calculate coalition strength
			OTT_calc_coalition_strength = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = -0.02 }
			change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		}
		LBA = {
			set_capital = { state = 663 remember_old_capital = no }
		}
		EGY = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				add_to_faction = LBA
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottsep.16 days = 70 }
		}
	}
}

			981 = {
				ott_set_authority_vilayet_medium = yes
				ott_increase_revolt_risk = yes
			}
		}
		752 = {
			ott_set_authority_vilayet_medium = yes
			ott_increase_revolt_risk = yes
		}
		982 = {
			ott_set_authority_vilayet_medium = yes
			ott_increase_revolt_risk = yes
		}
		659 = {
			ott_set_authority_vilayet_medium = yes
			ott_increase_revolt_risk = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = { hej_integration_factor = 5 tooltip = ott_increase_hej_int }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = hej_integration_factor
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
	}
}

		name = ottfor.13.a
		add_ideas = ott_balkan_military_accords
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = GRE
					tag = BUL
					tag = ALB
					tag = ROM
					tag = SER
				}
				OR = {
					is_subject = no
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = ottfor.14 hours = 4 random_hours = 4 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	#Balkan Military Accords - Partners React
	id = ottfor.14
	title = ottfor.14.t
	desc = ottfor.14.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.14 option ottfor.14.a"
		name = ottfor.14.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				original_tag = GRE
				has_idea = ott_greco_turkish_accord
			}
		}
		add_ideas = ott_balkan_military_accords
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { has_idea = ott_balkan_military_accords }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = non_aggression_pact
			}
		}

		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = GRE
					original_tag = BUL
					original_tag = ALB
					original_tag = ROM
					original_tag = SER
				}
				NOT = { has_idea = ott_balkan_military_accords }
			}
			country_event = { id = ottfor.14 hours = 4 random_hours = 4 }
		}
		FROM = { country_event = ottfor.15 }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.14 option ottfor.14.b"
		name = ottfor.14.b
		trigger = { compare_autonomy_state > default_puppet }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_subject_of = FROM
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		FROM = { country_event = ottfor.16 }
	}
}

country_event = {	#Istanbul Pact - Invite
	id = ottfor.18
	title = ottfor.18.t
	desc = ottfor.18.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.18 option ottfor.18.a"
		name = ottfor.18.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { tag = MOR }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = MOR_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = MOR_forpol option = MOR_FORPOL_OTT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = MOR_forpol option = MOR_FORPOL_VICTOR } }
			}
		}
		##check if the tag has a guarantee from GER (in order to fix issue of AZR losing its guarantee upon joining and locking OTT focus)
		if = {
			limit = { is_guaranteed_by = GER }
			set_country_flag = OTT_for_temp_has_guarantee
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
				var:FROM.faction_leader = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
			}
		}
		#readd GER guarantee to tag if it had it before
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = OTT_for_temp_has_guarantee }
			GER = { give_guarantee = AZR }
			clr_country_flag = OTT_for_temp_has_guarantee
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.18 option ottfor.18.b"
		name = ottfor.18.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				FROM = { tag = MOR }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = MOR_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = MOR_forpol option = MOR_FORPOL_OTT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = MOR_forpol option = MOR_FORPOL_VICTOR } }
			}
		}
		OTT = {
			country_event = ottfor.19
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
}

				factor = 0
				OR = {
					UKR = { is_in_faction_with = AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_forpol option = OTT_FORPOL_AUS }
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = ottfor.24 days = 14 }
		OTT = { country_event = { id = ottfor.24 days = 14 } }
	}

	option = { #Austria maintains its gaze on Eastern Europe

			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				UKR = { is_in_faction_with = AUS }
			}
		}
		OTT = { country_event = { id = ottfor.25 days = 7 } }
		add_war_support = 0.10
	}
}

country_event = {	#Ratification of the Sarajevo Accords
	id = ottfor.24
	title = ottfor.24.t
	desc = ottfor.24.d

	trigger = {
		is_valid_peace_target = yes
		AUS = { is_valid_peace_target = yes }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.24 option ottfor.24.a"
		name = ottfor.24.a
		set_country_flag = alliance_aus
		add_stability = 0.05
		complete_national_focus = OTT_Alliance_of_Convenience
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = no
				OR = {
					tag = SER
					tag = MNT
					tag = ALB
					tag = ROM
					tag = BUL
					tag = GRE
				}
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = AUS
					has_war_with = OTT
				}
			}
			PREV = { give_guarantee = PREV }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	#Meeting on Ada Kaleh
	id = ottfor.26
	title = ottfor.26.t
	desc = ottfor.26.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { tag = AUS }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
					set_faction_name = sarajevo_accords
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
					leave_faction = yes
					create_faction = sarajevo_accords
				}
				else = {
					create_faction = sarajevo_accords
				}
				every_other_country = {
					display_individual_scopes = yes
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = alliance_aus_accepted
							tag = OTT
						}
					}
					AUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.26 option ottfor.26.a"
		name = ottfor.26.a
		if = {
			limit = { tag = AUS }
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = AUS_protector_of_the_balkans } }
					complete_national_focus = AUS_protector_of_the_balkans
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				display_individual_scopes = yes
				limit = { has_country_flag = alliance_aus_accepted }
				custom_effect_tooltip = OTT_add_country_to_sarajevo_accords
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = OTT_add_ottomans_to_sarajevo_accords
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = {
			limit = {
				GRE = {
					is_in_faction_with = AUS
					has_country_flag = alliance_aus_accepted
				}
			}
			TUR = {
				remove_state_core = 187
				remove_state_core = 164
				remove_state_claim = 989
				if = {
					limit = { GRE = { owns_state = 769 } }
					remove_state_claim = 769
				}
			}
			GRE = {
				transfer_state = 187
				transfer_state = 164
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = ottfor.30.a

				factor = 0
				tag = SAU
			}
		}

			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				OR = {
					state = 347
					state = 656
					state = 907
					state = 993
					state = 658
				}
			}
			OTT = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.30 option ottfor.30.b"
		name = ottfor.30.b
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = OTT
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}

### Saudi-Oman Conflict
country_event = {	#Saudis encroach on the al-Buraimi Oasis
	id = ottfor.34
	title = ottfor.34.t
	desc = ottfor.34.d
	picture = GFX_OTT_Basra_Port

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.34 option ottfor.34.a"
		name = ottfor.34.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SAU_oman option = SAU_OMAN_ALONE }
			}
		}
		add_war_support = -0.10
		OMA = { country_event = { id = ottfor.35 days = 3 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = if_they_accept_tt
		effect_tooltip = { give_guarantee = OMA }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.34 option ottfor.34.b"
		name = ottfor.34.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = SAU_oman option = SAU_OMAN_OTT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = SAU_oman option = SAU_OMAN_RAJ }
				}
			}
		}
		save_event_target_as = OTT_abandoned_oman
		hidden_effect = {
			OMA = { country_event = { id = ottfor.35 days = 3 } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	#Ottomans offer 'protection' from the Saudi threat
	id = ottfor.35

	title = {
		text = ottfor.35.t.ottomans
		trigger = { NOT = { has_event_target = OTT_abandoned_oman } }
	}
	title = {
		text = ottfor.35.t.no_ottomans
		trigger = { has_event_target = OTT_abandoned_oman }
	}

	desc = {
		text = ottfor.35.d.ottomans
		trigger = { NOT = { has_event_target = OTT_abandoned_oman } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ottfor.35.d.no_ottomans
		trigger = { has_event_target = OTT_abandoned_oman }
	}

	picture = GFX_OTT_Dolmabahce

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.35 option ottfor.35.c"
		name = ottfor.35.c
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_event_target = OTT_abandoned_oman } }
			OTT = { country_event = { id = ottfor.37 days = 2 } }
		}
		unlock_national_focus = OMA_compromises_for_our_independence
		remove_ideas = has_scripted_peace
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.35 option ottfor.35.a"
		name = ottfor.35.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_event_target = OTT_abandoned_oman }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = SAU_oman option = SAU_OMAN_ALONE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = SAU_oman option = SAU_OMAN_RAJ }
				}
			}
		}
		OTT = {
			give_guarantee = OMA
			save_event_target_as = OMA_guarantor
			country_event = { id = ottfor.36 days = 2 }
		}
		effect_tooltip = { activate_mission = OMA_SAU_Whitepeace }
		SAU = { country_event = ottfor.410 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.35 option ottfor.35.b"
		name = ottfor.35.b
		trigger = {
			country_exists = RAJ
			NOT = { has_war_with = RAJ }
			RAJ = { is_subject = no }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = SAU_oman option = SAU_OMAN_ALONE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = SAU_oman option = SAU_OMAN_OTT }
				}
			}
		}
		RAJ = { country_event = { id = ottfor.38 days = 2 } }
	}
}

	desc = ottfor.36.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_battleship_kongo

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.36 option ottfor.36.a"
		name = ottfor.36.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { TUR = { has_completed_focus = OTT_Ottoman_Authority_Peninsula } }
			}
			effect_tooltip = { give_guarantee = OMA }
		}
		else = {
			OMA = { get_current_government_type = yes }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = OMA
				autonomy_state = nominal_puppet
				end_wars = no
			}
			OMA = { restore_previous_government_type = yes }
			OMA = { set_cosmetic_tag = OTT_client }
		}
	}
}

### Suez Canal
country_event = {	#The Port Said Straits Convention - OTT version
	id = ottfor.48
	title = ottfor.48.t
	desc = ottfor.48.d
	picture = GFX_OTT_Suez_Canal

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Create the Suez International Zone
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.48 option ottfor.48.a"
		name = ottfor.48.a
		trigger = {
			OTT_EGY_scripted_peace = yes
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		OTT_set_up_suez_canal_zone = yes
	}

	option = { #The Suez shall remain Turkish!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.48 option ottfor.48.b"
		name = ottfor.48.b
		trigger = {
			OTT_EGY_scripted_peace = no
		}
		set_global_flag = SUEZ_SUCCESS
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = AUS
					tag = NFA
					tag = CAN
					tag = ENT
					tag = GBR
					tag = SIC
					tag = HOL
					tag = BEL
					tag = GRE
				}
				has_socialist_government = no
				is_subject = no
				NOT = { has_war_with = OTT }
			}
			country_event = ottfor.50
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	#Russian Expansionism in the Caucasus - OTT pov
	id = ottfor.51
	title = ottfor.51.t
	desc = ottfor.51.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_tanks

	trigger = {
		tag = OTT
		country_exists = GEO
		country_exists = AZR
		RUS = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
		}
		NOT = {
			is_in_faction_with = GER
			is_in_faction_with = ENT
			has_completed_focus = OTT_Abolish_Full_Neutrality
			#has_completed_focus = OTT_Abolish_Full_Neutrality_Fevzi
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = OTT_baku_conference_ongoing
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.51 option ottfor.51.a"
		name = ottfor.51.a	# OTT proposes NAP
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_RUS_convention option = OTT_RUS_CONVENTION_FAILURE }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_forpol option = OTT_FORPOL_OTT } }
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = ottfor.55
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.51 option ottfor.51.b"
		name = ottfor.51.b	# RUS gets chance to propose NAP
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		RUS = {
			country_event = ottfor.53
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	#The Baku Conference
	id = ottfor.56
	title = ottfor.56.t
	desc = ottfor.56.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference

	trigger = {
		OTT_russo_ottoman_convention_can_proceed = yes
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.56 option ottfor.56.a"
		name = ottfor.56.a
		if = {
			limit = { #if Georgia is invalid, skip to Afghanistan
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = GEO }
					RUS = { is_ally_with = GEO }
					RUS = { has_war_with = GEO }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { #if Afghanistan is invalid, skip to Persia
					OR = {
						NOT = { country_exists = AFG }
						RUS = { is_ally_with = AFG }
						RUS = { has_war_with = AFG }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { tag = OTT }
					country_event = { id = ottfor.66 days = 2 }
				}
				else = {
					effect_tooltip = {
						OTT = { country_event = { id = ottfor.66 days = 2 } }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { tag = RUS }
					country_event = { id = ottfor.63 days = 2 }
				}
				else = {
					effect_tooltip = {
						RUS = { country_event = { id = ottfor.63 days = 2 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = RUS }
				country_event = { id = ottfor.57 days = 2 }
			}
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					RUS = { country_event = { id = ottfor.57 days = 2 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	#Russia Demands Georgian Annexation
	id = ottfor.58
	title = ottfor.58.t
	desc = ottfor.58.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference

	trigger = {
		OTT_russo_ottoman_convention_can_proceed = yes
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.58 option ottfor.58.a"
		name = ottfor.58.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		set_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL_GEO_ANNEX
		if = {
			limit = { #if OTT does not own Batumi, skip to Afghanistan
				NOT = { owns_state = 585 } #Batumi
			}
			if = {
				limit = { #if Afghanistan is invalid, skip to Persia
					OR = {
						NOT = { country_exists = AFG }
						RUS = { is_ally_with = AFG }
						RUS = { has_war_with = AFG }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottfor.66 days = 2 }
			}
			else = {
				RUS = { country_event = { id = ottfor.63 days = 2 } }
			}
		}
		else = {
			RUS = { country_event = { id = ottfor.61 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.58 option ottfor.58.b"
		name = ottfor.58.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		RUS = { country_event = { id = ottfor.60 days = 1 } }
	}
}

country_event = {	#Russia Demands Batumi
	id = ottfor.62
	title = ottfor.62.t
	desc = ottfor.62.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference

	trigger = {
		OTT_russo_ottoman_convention_can_proceed = yes
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.62 option ottfor.62.a"
		name = ottfor.62.a				# Yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				surrender_progress > 0.2
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				surrender_progress > 0.4
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_RUS_convention option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_RUS_convention option = OTT_RUS_CONVENTION_FAILURE } }
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL_BATUMI
		if = {
			limit = { #if Afghanistan is invalid, skip to Persia
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = AFG }
					RUS = { is_ally_with = AFG }
					RUS = { has_war_with = AFG }
					AFG = { has_capitulated = yes }
				}
			}
			OTT = { country_event = { id = ottfor.66 days = 2 } }
		}
		else = {
			RUS = { country_event = { id = ottfor.63 days = 2 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.62 option ottfor.62.b"
		name = ottfor.62.b			# No
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				add = -50
				surrender_progress > 0.2
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -50
				surrender_progress > 0.4
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -100

			}
		}
		RUS = { country_event = { id = ottfor.60 days = 1 } }
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference

		OTT_russo_ottoman_convention_can_proceed = yes
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.67 option ottfor.67.a"
		name = ottfor.67.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				RUS_is_expansionist = yes
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_RUS_convention option = OTT_RUS_CONVENTION_SUCCESS_OTT } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_RUS_convention option = OTT_RUS_CONVENTION_SUCCESS_RUS }
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL_PER_BUFFER
		if = {
			limit = { #if Azerbaijan is invalid, skip to straits convention
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = AZR }
					is_ally_with = AZR
					has_war_with = AZR
					AZR = { has_capitulated = yes }
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = ottfor.73 days = 1 }
		}
		else = {
			OTT = { country_event = { id = ottfor.71 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.67 option ottfor.67.b"
		name = ottfor.67.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				RUS_is_expansionist = no
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_RUS_convention option = OTT_RUS_CONVENTION_SUCCESS_RUS } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_RUS_convention option = OTT_RUS_CONVENTION_SUCCESS_OTT }
			}
		}
		OTT = { country_event = { id = ottfor.69 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.67 option ottfor.67.c"
		name = ottfor.67.c
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		OTT = { country_event = { id = ottfor.60 days = 1 } }
	}
}

	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.77 option ottfor.77.a"
		name = ottfor.77.a
		set_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL
		clr_global_flag = OTT_baku_conference_ongoing

			limit = { tag = RUS }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = "OTT"
				value = 200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = conquer
				id = "OTT"
				value = -200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL_AZR_BUFFER }
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = "AZR"
					value = 200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = conquer
					id = "AZR"
					value = -200
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = "RUS"
				value = 200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = conquer
				id = "RUS"
				value = -200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL_AZR_BUFFER }
				AZR = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = befriend
						id = "RUS"
						value = 200
					}
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = conquer
						id = "RUS"
						value = -200
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Clear RUS AI factors once Germany is dead or ten years have passed
	id = ottfor.771
	title = ottfor.771.t

	desc = {
		text = ottfor.771.d.TUR_war
		trigger = {
			original_tag = TUR
			has_war_with = RUS
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ottfor.771.d.TUR_russia_dead
		trigger = {
			original_tag = TUR
			NOT = { has_war_with = RUS }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ottfor.771.d.RUS_war
		trigger = {
			original_tag = RUS
			has_war_with = TUR
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ottfor.771.d.RUS_turkey_dead
		trigger = {
			original_tag = RUS
			NOT = { has_war_with = TUR }
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.771 option ottfor.771.a"
		name = ottfor.771.a
		AZR = { remove_ideas = OTT_russo_ottoman_convention }
		RUS = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_guaranteed = OTT }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = OTT
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = OTT }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = OTT
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_military_access_to = OTT }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = OTT
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { gives_military_access_to = OTT }
				OTT = {
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ROOT
						relation = military_access
						active = no
					}
				}
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = "OTT"
				value = -200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = conquer
				id = "OTT"
				value = 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL_AZR_BUFFER }
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = "AZR"
					value = -200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = conquer
					id = "AZR"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = 266.ambition_area_@ROOT }
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = PER.core_states
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = ambition_area_@ROOT } }
					set_variable = { ambition_area_@ROOT = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		OTT = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = "RUS"
				value = -200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = conquer
				id = "RUS"
				value = 200
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL_AZR_BUFFER }
			AZR = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = "RUS"
					value = -200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = conquer
					id = "RUS"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		OTT_clear_russo_ottoman_convention_effect = yes
	}
}

country_event = {	#Russia Demands an End to Hostilities
	id = ottfor.79
	title = ottfor.79.t
	desc = ottfor.79.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL_PER_BUFFER
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.79 option ottfor.79.a"
		name = ottfor.79.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war_with = RUS
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		every_subject_country = {
			overlord = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PREV
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
			}
		}
		separate_peace_all_wars = yes
		add_ideas = generic_neutral_foreign_policy
	}
	option = {

				add = 100

			}

				add = 20
				RUS = { has_war_with = GER }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RUS = { can_declare_war_on = ROOT } }
			RUS = {
				create_wargoal = {
					target = ROOT
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}

		name = ottfor.80.a

		add_ideas = generic_neutral_foreign_policy
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		separate_peace_all_wars = yes
		GER = {
			remove_resource_rights = 229
			if = {
				limit = { has_military_access_to = ROOT }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_guaranteed_by = GER }
			GER = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		OTT = {
			give_guarantee = ROOT
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = non_aggression_pact
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			give_guarantee = ROOT
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = non_aggression_pact
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.80 option ottfor.80.b"
		name = ottfor.80.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		RUS = {
			create_wargoal = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			GER = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	#The Russo-Ottoman Convention
	id = ottfor.83
	title = ottfor.83.t
	desc = ottfor.83.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL
		RUS = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
		OTT = {
			exists = yes
			is_subject = no
			has_capitulated = no
			NOT = { has_war_with = RUS }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.83 option ottfor.83.a"
		name = ottfor.83.a
		### Persia
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = PER }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = RUSSIAN_OTTOMAN_DEAL_PER_SPLIT }
				413 = { #Khuzestan
					if = {
						limit = { owner = { is_ally_with = RUS } }
						transfer_state_to = OTT
					}
				}
				417 = { #Urmia
					if = {
						limit = { owner = { is_ally_with = RUS } }
						transfer_state_to = OTT
					}
				}
				419 = { #Tabriz
					if = {
						limit = { owner = { is_ally_with = RUS } }
						transfer_state_to = OTT
					}
				}
				421 = { #Kermanshah
					if = {
						limit = { owner = { is_ally_with = RUS } }
						transfer_state_to = OTT
					}
				}
				PER = {
					every_core_state = {
						limit = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									is_ally_with = TUR
									is_ally_with = RUS
								}
							}
							NOT = { is_core_of = owner }
							NOT = { is_claimed_by = owner }
							NOT = { state = 413 } #Khuzestan
							NOT = { state = 417 } #Urmia
							NOT = { state = 419 } #Tabriz
							NOT = { state = 421 } #Kermanshah
						}
						transfer_state_to = PER
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				PER = {
					every_core_state = {
						limit = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									is_ally_with = TUR
									is_ally_with = RUS
								}
							}
							NOT = { is_core_of = owner }
							NOT = { is_claimed_by = owner }
						}
						transfer_state_to = PER
					}
					add_ideas = generic_neutral_foreign_policy
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_socialist_government = yes
								has_government = national_populist
							}
						}
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
							elections_allowed = no
						}
						set_political_party = {
							ideology = authoritarian_democrat
							popularity = 60
						}
					}
				}
				OTT = { give_guarantee = PER }
				RUS = { give_guarantee = PER }
			}
		}
		### Azerbaijan
		else = {
			AZR = {
				every_core_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								is_ally_with = TUR
								is_ally_with = RUS
							}
						}
						NOT = { is_core_of = owner }
						NOT = { is_claimed_by = owner }
					}
					transfer_state_to = AZR
				}
				add_ideas = generic_neutral_foreign_policy
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_socialist_government = yes
							has_government = national_populist
						}
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					set_political_party = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						popularity = 60
					}
				}
			}
			OTT = { give_guarantee = PER }
			RUS = { give_guarantee = PER }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	#A Kaiser, a Sultan, and a Tsar
	id = ottfor.87
	title = ottfor.87.t
	desc = {
		text = ottfor.87.d_friend_won
		trigger = {
			THIS = {
				has_completed_focus = BUL_kostantiniye_diplomacy
				has_completed_focus = BUL_balkan_war_victory
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ottfor.87.d_lost
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = BUL_balkan_war_defeat
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ottfor.87.d_enemy_won
		trigger = {
			#WIPhas_completed_focus = BUL_balkan_war_victory
			any_core_state = { is_owned_by = FROM }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_BUL_palace

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #join sarajevo gang
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.87 option ottfor.87.a"
		name = ottfor.87.a
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = BUL_balkan_war_victory
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }

		OTT = {
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ottfor.90 days = 1 } }
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = AUS }
				AUS = { add_to_faction = BUL }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = alliance_aus_accepted
		BUL = {
			if = {
				limit = { var:184.owner = { is_ally_with = OTT } }
				transfer_state = 184 #Komotini
			}
			if = {
				limit = { var:1089.owner = { is_ally_with = OTT } }
				transfer_state = 1089 #Kardzhali
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #join sarajevo gang
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.87 option ottfor.87.b"
		name = ottfor.87.b
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = BUL_balkan_war_defeat
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }

		OTT = {
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ottfor.90 days = 1 } }
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = AUS }
				AUS = { add_to_faction = BUL }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = alliance_aus_accepted
	}

	option = { #reject sarajevo gang
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.87 option ottfor.87.c"
		name = ottfor.87.c
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }

		FROM = { country_event = { id = ottfor.901 days = 1 } }
	}
}

			229 = { is_owned_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes }
			230 = { is_owned_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes }
			231 = { is_owned_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes }
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				surrender_progress > 0.30
				OR = {
					var:229.controller = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
					var:230.controller = { is_ally_with = ROOT }

			}

				234 = { is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = no }

### Ottoman - Egyptian stalemate scripted peace
country_event = { #Peace with Egypt?
	id = ottfor.96
	title = ottfor.96.t
	desc = ottfor.96.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_EGY_egyptian_palace

	trigger = {
		tag = OTT
		has_war_with = EGY
		is_valid_peace_target = yes

		#Egypt has lost initiative and has been pushed to the Suez
		EGY = {
			is_valid_peace_target = yes
			has_idea = EGY_levant_crisis_initiative_lost
			#All faction members in the Middle East have capitulated
			NOT = {
				any_allied_country = {
					is_in_middle_east = yes
					has_capitulated = no
				}
			}
			controls_state = 446 #Cairo
			NOT = { controls_state = 453 } #Sinai
			#Eastern bank of the Suez
			NOT = { controls_province = 1155 }
			NOT = { controls_province = 9947 }
		}

		#Ottomans are either under immediate threat, or too war-weary
		OR = {
			casualties_k > 250
			AND = {
				has_war_support < 0.2
				has_manpower < 10000
			}
			surrender_progress > 0.39
			AND = {
				owns_state = 773 #Constantinople
				NOT = { controls_state = 773 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_war_with = PER
				#OTT has been pushed out of Iraq and some
				NOT = { controls_state = 291 } #Baghdad
				NOT = { controls_state = 676 } #Mosul
				OR = {
					NOT = { controls_state = 350 } #Diyarbakir
					NOT = { controls_state = 352 } #Van
					NOT = { controls_state = 354 } #Erzurum
					NOT = { controls_state = 677 } #Aleppo
				}
			}
			var:global.russia = {
				at_war_with_or_justifying_wargoal_against_ROOT = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = OTT_Union_Party_State } #Kadro-proofing
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Let's end this
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.96 option ottfor.96.a"
		name = ottfor.96.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = OTT_EGY_scripted_peace_warning_tt
		EGY = { country_event = ottfor.97 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = if_they_accept_tt
		event_option_tooltip = ottfor.98.a
	}

	option = { #No chance
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottfor.96 option ottfor.96.b"
		name = ottfor.96.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}
}

	id = ottlib.20
	title = ottlib.20.t
	desc = ottlib.20.d

	#picture = GFX_OTT_Kazim_Speech

	trigger = {
		social_liberal_plurality = yes
		has_completed_focus = OTT_Grand_Vizier_Sabahaddin
		has_completed_focus = OTT_Multi_Level_Democracy
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottlib.20 option ottlib.20.a"
		name = ottlib.20.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_MARLIB }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCCON }
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		activate_advisor = TUR_musa_kazim_karabekir_sic
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_temp_unit_leader_role = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottlib.20 option ottlib.20.b"
		name = ottlib.20.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCLIB }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -75
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_temp_unit_leader_role = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	#Coup in Baghdad
	id = ottlib.21
	title = ottlib.21.t
	desc = ottlib.21.d

	picture = GFX_IRQ_Tank_Street

	trigger = {
		controls_state = 291
		owns_state = 676
		has_war_with = EGY
		has_democratic_government = yes
		has_country_flag = yasin_goes_yeet
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;Iraq REVOLTS AGAINST OTT"
		hidden_effect = {
			291 = { teleport_armies = { limit = { is_ally_with = ROOT } to_state = 350 } }
			676 = { teleport_armies = { limit = { is_ally_with = ROOT } to_state = 350 } }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottlib.21 option ottlib.21.a"
		name = ottlib.21.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_character = IRQ_yasin_al_hashimi }
				IRQ_yasin_al_hashimi = { set_nationality = IRQ }
			}
		}
		IRQ = {
			hidden_effect = {
				transfer_technology_without_doctrines = yes
				IRQ_yasin_al_hashimi = {
					set_nationality = PREV
					promote_character = yes
					promote_to_field_marshal = yes
				}
			}
			activate_advisor = IRQ_taha_al_hashimi_sic
			transfer_state = 676
			transfer_state = 291
			IRQ_spawn_initial_units = yes
			declare_war_on = {
				target = OTT
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		EGY = { add_to_faction = IRQ }
	}
}

country_event = {	#Elections 1940
	id = ottlib.22
	title = ottlib.22.t
	desc = ottlib.22.d

	picture = GFX_OTT_Sublime_Porte1

	trigger = {
		date > 1938.01.01
		OR = {
			has_government = social_liberal
			has_government = market_liberal
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = ott_centralist_DF
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottlib.22 option ottlib.22.a"
		name = ottlib.22.a
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 0.05 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = seats_redistributed

		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = ohf_deputies
			value = 30
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = hif_deputies
			value = 30
		}

		clamp_variable = {
			var = ohf_deputies
			min = 0
			max = 500
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = hif_deputies
			min = 0
			max = 500
		}

		### Calculate coalition strength
		OTT_calc_coalition_strength = yes
	}
}

country_event = {	#Nationalists Celebrate Conquest of Western Thrace
	id = ottlib.24

	title = ottlib.24.t

	desc = ottlib.24.d

	picture = GFX_OTT_Kardzhali

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		owns_state = 184
		owns_state = 1089
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = BUL
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottlib.24 option ottlib.24.a"
		name = ottlib.24.a

		if = {
			limit = { OTT_has_centralist_government = no }
			### Add Turkish Nationalist votes in favour
			add_to_variable = { nat_tur_sup_deputies = 10 tooltip = nat_tur_sup_tt }
			### Calculate coalition strength
			OTT_calc_coalition_strength = yes
			add_political_power = 25
		}
		else = {

			### Increase Stability
			add_stability = 0.05
			add_political_power = 25
		}
	}
}

			state = 676
		}

				NOT = { has_war_with = OTT }
				num_of_factories > 35
				is_subject = no
				has_socialist_government = no
				any_owned_state = {
					is_coastal = yes
				}
			}
			country_event = otteco.7
		}

			limit = { OTT_has_centralist_government = no }

			OTT_calc_coalition_strength = yes
		}
	}

		### Return Conservative votes to opposition
		subtract_from_variable = { con_sup_deputies = 30 tooltip = con_opp_tt }

		### Add Turkish Nationalist votes in favour
		add_to_variable = { nat_tur_sup_deputies = 10 tooltip = nat_tur_sup_tt }

		### Calculate coalition strength
		OTT_calc_coalition_strength = yes
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottsab.35 option ottsab.35.b"
		name = ottsab.35.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = OTT_path option = OTT_PATH_SOCCON }
			}
		}
	}
}

unit_leader_event = {	#Coup d'État in Kostantiniye
	id = ottars.11
	title = ottars.11.t
	desc = ottars.11.d

	#picture = GFX_OTT_Troops_Istanbul

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ottars.11 option ottars.11.a"
		name = ottars.11.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
			name = TUR_military_government
			long_name = TUR_military_government_long
		}
		end_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = { TUR_fevzi_cakmak = { set_nationality = ROOT } }
		activate_advisor = TUR_fevzi_cakmak_sic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottfev.1 days = 3 }
			country_event = { id = ottfev.6 days = 14 }
			news_event = ottnews.3
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = EGY
						is_core_of = SUD
						is_core_of = ARM
						is_core_of = LBA
						is_core_of = TRP
						is_core_of = YEM
						is_core_of = HEJ
					}
				}
				clear_occupy_state = yes
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = ott_military_purge
		load_focus_tree = ottoman_fevzi_coup_focus
		complete_national_focus = OTT_State_of_Emergency
		set_stability = 0.6
		OTT_remove_kemalist_ideas = yes
	}
}

	id = ottnews.1

	desc = ottnews.1.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

		wants_world_news = yes
	}

		regional_middle_east_news = yes
	}

		name = ottnews.1.a
	}
}
